Scotturb Bus 403 is a bus route operated by Scotturb in Lisbon, Portugal. It runs from the city centre to Sintra, passing through the towns of Cascais, Estoril, and Cabo da Roca.
The route is operated by a fleet of 12 Mercedes-Benz Citaros.

Catalan is the official language of Catalonia, a region in northeastern Spain. It is spoken by about 7.5 million people, and is the native language of about 75% of the population.
The Catalan language is a Romance language, and is closely related to the languages of the other Romance languages, such as French, Italian, and Spanish.
Catalan is a very phonetic language, and is very easy to learn. It is also very similar to Spanish, and is often used as a second language in Spain.

The Metro is a rapid transit system serving the city of Barcelona, Spain. It is operated by the Metro de Barcelona, a public transport company owned by the Generalitat of Catalonia.
The Metro is the second-longest metro system in Spain, after the Madrid Metro, and the 11th-longest in Europe. It has 75 stations and 142 km (88.7 mi) of track.
The Metro is the most used public transport system in Barcelona, with 1.2 million passengers per day
